        function cdnfallback() {
            if (window.appInsights) {
                var region = "UK South";
                var siteName = "acom-prod-uksouth-02";
                var error = new Error('Bundle - client side cdn fallback to local cdn, region: ' + region + ' , sitename: ' + siteName);

                window.appInsights.trackException({ exception: error });
            }

            if (window.location.search.indexOf('cdn=disable') === -1) {
                window.location.href = '?cdn=disable';
            }
        }

  <script>

    $(window).on('load', function () {
        function enableSSO() {
            setTimeout(function () {
                window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
                var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                iframe.src = '/auth/sso/';
                iframe.setAttribute('id', 'sso-frame');
                iframe.setAttribute('style', 'width: 0; height: 0; border: 0; border: none; position: absolute;');
                iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
                $('body').prepend(iframe);
            }, 500);
        }

        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin !== 'https://azure.microsoft.com' || event.data !== 'sso-success') {
            return;
            }

            
            window.setTimeout(function () { document.getElementById('sso-frame').contentWindow.location.replace('/auth/sso/'); }, 30 * 60 * 1000);

            
            var enabledSubmitInputs = $('input:enabled[type="submit"], button:enabled[type="submit"]');
            enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', true);

            window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.success')); 

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/sso/info/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    if (data) {
                        $('.auth-container').html(data);
                    }
                })
                .fail(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/antiforgerytoken/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').replaceWith(data);
                    window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.requestVerificationTokenReceived'));
                })
                .always(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });
        }

        
        function createNewEvent(eventName) {
            var event;

            if (typeof (Event) === 'function') {
                event = new Event(eventName);
            } else {
                event = document.createEvent('Event'); 
                event.initEvent(eventName, true, true);
            }

            return event;
        }

        // We won't process requests made from any status page
        if (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/status/') === -1)
        {
            // enable sso only if the userAgent is not safari
            if (!/^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                enableSSO();
            }
        }
    });

</script>

    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-3"> 
      <h2>Choose the right VM for your workload and reduce costs</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-6"> 
      <p> Migrate your business- and mission-critical workloads to <a href="/en-us/overview/what-is-azure/iaas/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">Azure infrastructure</a> and improve operational efficiency. Run <a href="/en-us/services/virtual-machines/sql-server/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">SQL Server</a>, <a href="/en-us/solutions/sap/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">SAP</a>, <a href="/en-us/solutions/oracle/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">Oracle</a><sup></sup> software and <a href="/en-us/solutions/high-performance-computing/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">high-performance computing</a> applications on Azure Virtual Machines. Choose your favorite <a href="/en-us/services/virtual-machines/linux/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">Linux</a> distribution or <a href="/en-us/services/virtual-machines/windows/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">Windows Server</a>. </p> 
      <p>Deploy virtual machines featuring up to 416 vCPUs and 12 TB of memory. Get up to 3.7 million local storage IOPS per VM. Take advantage of up to 30 Gbps Ethernet and clouds first deployment of 200 Gbps InfiniBand.</p> <a href="/en-us/pricing/details/virtual-machines/series/" class="arrow-link" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-vmseries">Explore the full list of Azure VM types</a> 
     </div>

   <section class="section" aria-label="Optimize your infrastructure and save money as well as govern, monitor, and back up your VM environments."> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-8 medium-offset-1 medium-push-3">

     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-3 medium-pull-9"> 
      <h2>Optimize your infrastructure and save money</h2> 
      <p> Reduce costsup to 72 percent compared to pay-as-you-go priceswith term pricing through <a href="/en-us/pricing/reserved-vm-instances/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">Azure Reserved Virtual Machine Instances</a>. Re-use your on-premises licenses to run Windows Server VMs on Azure with <a href="/en-us/pricing/hybrid-benefit/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">Azure Hybrid Benefit</a> and combine RIs with Azure Hybrid Benefit to save up to 80 percent. Take advantage of <a href="https://aka.ms/SpotVMPage" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">spot pricing</a> on Azure VMs and VMSS to run interruptible workloads at deep discounts compared to pay as you go rates. Optimize your cloud spend with <a href="/en-us/services/cost-management/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">Azure Cost Management</a>. Get three more years of free extended security updates for Windows Server 2008 and 2008 R2 when you migrate to Azure. </p> 
      <p><a class="arrow-link" href="/en-us/pricing/hybrid-benefit/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-ahb">Discover why Azure is the most cost-effective cloud for Windows Server</a></p>

       <h3> Azure Dedicated Hostyour very own private cloud in Azure </h3> 
       <p>Use Azure Dedicated Host to control the maintenance window, gain visibility over the underlying infrastructure, and place your Azure VMs on a single tenant server to satisfy specific compliance or regulatory requirements.</p> <a class="arrow-link" href="/en-us/resources/videos/azure-dedicated-host-your-very-own-private-cloud-in-azure/">Watch the video</a>

     <div class="column medium-8 medium-offset-1 medium-push-3"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/virtual-machines/portal-advisor-recommendations.jpg" class="device-wrapper" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-3 medium-pull-9"> 
      <h2>Govern, monitor, and back up your VM environments</h2> 
      <p>Ensure compliance and deploy applications to production faster across your entire business with <a href="/en-us/services/blueprints/">Azure Blueprints</a>. Get recommendations for high availability, security, performance, and cost for all of your VMs with <a href="/en-us/services/advisor/">Azure Advisor</a>. Safeguard your data against ransomware with <a href="/en-us/services/backup/">Azure Backup</a>. Proactively identify issues and gain intelligent insights with <a href="/en-us/services/monitor/">Azure Monitor</a>.</p> <a class="arrow-link" href="/en-us/services/azure-policy/">Control your resources with Azure Policy</a> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row column"> <a href="/en-us/blog/amd-based-memory-optimized-azure-virtual-machines-now-available-in-more-regions/" class="card--announcement" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-announcement"> <span class="card--announcement__text">Expanded availability for AMD-based memory-optimized Azure Virtual Machines</span> </a> 
    </div> 
   </div> 
   <div class="section section-size6"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-6"> 
      <div class="row column"> 
       <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/virtual-machines/dashboard.jpg" alt=""> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row row-size2 column"> 
       <p class="text-heading3">Embrace consistent hybrid cloud technologies</p> 
       <p> Extend the capacity of your datacenter with Azure VMs and access on-demand, high-performance computing capabilities in the cloud. Develop, test, run, and operate <a href="/en-us/overview/hybrid-cloud/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">hybrid cloud</a> applications consistently across Azure and your on-premises environment. Adopt simple and cost-effective cloud backup and <a href="https://aka.ms/BCDR-ACOM-page" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-link">disaster recovery solutions</a> to avoid business interruptions. Meet regulatory and policy requirements for your VMs by developing in Azure and deploying on premises with Azure Stack. </p> <a href="/en-us/overview/azure-stack/" class="arrow-link">Learn more Azure Stack</a> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-6"> 
      <div class="row column"> 
       <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/virtual-machines/cray-sentinel.jpg" alt=""> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row row-size2 column"> 
       <p class="text-heading3">Scale your infrastructure without adding complexity</p> 
       <p>Set up highly available, centrally managed, and scalable services for computationally intensive, big data, and container workloads with <a href="/en-us/services/virtual-machine-scale-sets/">VM scale sets</a>. Reduce cost and time to reimage your VMs for your stateless applications with <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/ephemeral-os-disks">Ephemeral OS disks</a>. Manage global replication and sharing of images at scale with <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/shared-image-galleries">shared image galleries</a>. Use <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/generation-2">generation 2 VMs</a> to improve boot and installation times. Get extreme computing power for your artificial intelligence (AI) and remote visualization workloads with GPU-enabled VMs.</p> <a href="/en-us/solutions/high-performance-computing/" class="arrow-link">Learn more about high-performance computing on Azure</a> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div>

    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-8 medium-offset-1 medium-push-3"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/virtual-machines/portal-security-center.jpg" class="device-wrapper" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-3 medium-pull-9"> 
      <h2>Enhance security and compliance</h2> 
      <p>Protect your VMs against bootkits, rootkits, and kernel-level malware with <a href="https://aka.ms/trustedlaunch">trusted launch</a>. Safeguard your VM data while in use with <a href="/en-us/solutions/confidential-compute/">Azure confidential computing</a>. Monitor your workloads and find and fix vulnerabilities with <a href="/en-us/services/security-center/">Azure Security Center</a>. Meet a broad set of international and industry-specific compliance standards, including General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR), ISO 27001, HIPAA, FedRAMP, and SOC 2. Deploy your Azure VMs on <a href="/en-us/services/virtual-machines/dedicated-host/">Azure Dedicated Host</a>, a physical server used only by your organization. Take advantage of a broad range of <a href="/en-us/support/legal/sla/virtual-machines/">VM service level agreements (SLAs)</a>: from single-instance VMs at 99.9 percent, up to 99.99 percent for VMs deployed across two or more Azure Availability Zones.</p> <a class="arrow-link" href="/en-us/services/virtual-machines/security/" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-security">Learn more about protecting your VMs</a> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section>

   <section class="section" aria-label="Documentation, training, and migration resources" id="documentation"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="medium-3 column"> 
      <h2>Documentation, training, and migration resources</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="medium-5 column"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4 text-center">5-minute quickstarts</h3> 
      <div class="row"> 
       <div class="medium-5 column"> 
        <h4 class="text-heading6">Linux</h4> 
        <p>Build an NGINX web-server within an Ubuntu VM using:</p> 
        <ul class="list--links" aria-label="Linux"> 
         <li><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/quick-create-cli" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-resourcelink">Azure CLI</a></li> 
         <li><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/quick-create-portal" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-resourcelink">Azure portal</a></li> 
         <li><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/quick-create-powershell" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-resourcelink">Azure PowerShell</a></li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
       <div class="medium-5 medium-offset-2 column"> 
        <h4 class="text-heading6">Windows</h4> 
        <p>Build an IIS web server within a Windows Server 2016 VM using:</p> 
        <ul class="list--links" aria-label="Windows"> 
         <li><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/quick-create-cli" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-resourcelink">Azure CLI</a></li> 
         <li><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/quick-create-portal" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-resourcelink">Azure portal</a></li> 
         <li><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/quick-create-powershell" data-event="area-products-details-clicked-resourcelink">Azure PowerShell</a></li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="medium-3 column"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4">Learning modules</h3>

      <ul class="list--links" aria-label="Learning modules">

      </ul> 
     </div>

    <div class="row row-size4">

   <section class="section" id="faqs" aria-label="Frequently asked questions about Azure and Azure VMs"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-3"> 
      <div class="row column"> 
       <h2>Frequently asked questions about Azure and Azure VMs</h2> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row column"> 
       <ul class="list--links"> 
        <li><a href="/en-us/global-infrastructure/services/?products=virtual-machines" data-event="global-panel-getstarted-clicked-link">Product availability by region</a></li> 
        <li><a href="https://status.azure.com/" data-event="global-panel-getstarted-clicked-link">Current operational status</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/en-us/support/legal/sla/virtual-machines/" data-event="global-panel-getstarted-clicked-link">Service-level agreement (SLA)</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-8 medium-offset-1"> 
      <ul class="faq"> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="6f50273b" data-bi-slot="1" data-bi-id="faq-1" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What are Azure Virtual Machines? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="6f50273b">
         <p>Azure Virtual Machines are image service instances that provide on-demand and scalable computing resources with usage-based pricing.</p> 
         <p>More broadly, a virtual machine behaves like a server: It's a computer within a computer that provides the user the same experience they would have on the host operating system itself. In general, virtual machines are sandboxed from the rest of the system, meaning that the software inside a virtual machine cant escape or tamper with the underlying server itself.</p> 
         <p>Each virtual machine provides its own virtual hardware including CPUs, memory, hard drives, network interfaces, and other devices.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="c9482411" data-bi-slot="2" data-bi-id="faq-2" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Which on-premises servers can be migrated to Azure? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="c9482411">
         <p>A range of guest operating systems, including the Azure-endorsed <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/endorsed-distros?toc=%2Fazure%2Fvirtual-machines%2Flinux%2Ftoc.json">Linux</a> and <a href="https://support.microsoft.com/help/2721672/microsoft-server-software-support-for-microsoft-azure-virtual-machines">Windows Server versions</a> can be migrated to Azure. Migrate physical servers or virtual machines from <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/migrate/server-migrate-overview">VMware environments</a> and <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/migrate/tutorial-prepare-hyper-v">Microsoft Hyper-V environments</a> with <a href="/en-us/services/azure-migrate/">Azure Migrate</a>. VMs migrated from these on-premises virtualization platforms run as native Azure infrastructure as a service (IaaS) VMs and aren't dependent on the on-premises hypervisor.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="f81580d2" data-bi-slot="3" data-bi-id="faq-3" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What is a vCPU? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="f81580d2">
         <p>vCPU stands for virtual central processing unit. A vCPU is a share of a physical CPU that is assigned to a virtual machine. An Azure VM can contain one or more vCPUs.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="39f79bed" data-bi-slot="4" data-bi-id="faq-4" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Do Azure VMs support hyperthreading? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="39f79bed">
         <p>Some Azure Virtual Machines support hyperthreading. Hyperthreading improves parallelization of computations performed on x86 microprocessors. For each physical processor core, the operating system addresses two virtual cores and shares the workload between them. A list of Azure VMs supporting hyperthreading is available in <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/acu">Azure Virtual Machines documentation</a>.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="1e5ce600" data-bi-slot="5" data-bi-id="faq-5" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Which operating systems does Azure support? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="1e5ce600">
         <p>In addition to various <a href="https://support.microsoft.com/help/2721672/microsoft-server-software-support-for-microsoft-azure-virtual-machines">Windows Server versions</a>, Azure supports all the major <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/endorsed-distros?toc=%2Fazure%2Fvirtual-machines%2Flinux%2Ftoc.json">Linux distributions</a>, including Red Hat Enterprise Linux, CentOS, CoreOS, Debian, Oracle Linux, SUSE Linux Enterprise, openSUSE, and Ubuntu.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="77129b7f" data-bi-slot="6" data-bi-id="faq-6" data-bi-an="faq-01"> How many different VM types are available on Azure and what type of workloads can they run? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="77129b7f">
         <p>Azure offers a range of virtual machinestheres a VM for every workload. <a href="/en-us/pricing/details/virtual-machines/series/">View the entire set of Azure Virtual Machine Series</a> or read the documentation for <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/sizes">Linux VMs</a> or <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/sizes">Windows VMs</a> to learn more.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__button-container faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question faq__load-more-button">Load more FAQs</button> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="13cce94c" data-bi-slot="7" data-bi-id="faq-7" data-bi-an="faq-01"> How can I find out which VM best fits my workload? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="13cce94c">
         <p>The <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines">Azure VM technical documentation pages</a>, <a href="/en-us/pricing/details/virtual-machines/series/">Azure VM series pages</a>, and <a href="/en-us/pricing/calculator/?service=virtual-machines">Azure VM pricing calculator</a> can help you determine your VM needs.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="8685fb0e" data-bi-slot="8" data-bi-id="faq-8" data-bi-an="faq-01"> How can I check the regional availability of a specific VM series and size? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="8685fb0e">
         <a href="/en-us/global-infrastructure/services/">See Azure product availability by region.</a>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="c245bc82" data-bi-slot="9" data-bi-id="faq-9" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What is an Azure Compute Unit and why is it important? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="c245bc82">
         <p>The concept of <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/acu">Azure Compute Units</a> (ACUs) provides a way of comparing compute (CPU) performance across Azure VM sizes. This helps to easily identify which Azure VM is most likely to satisfy your performance requirements. ACU is currently standardized on a Small (Standard_A1) VM being 100, with higher numbers representing approximately how much faster those products can run a standard benchmark.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="5c6dad44" data-bi-slot="10" data-bi-id="faq-10" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What tools are available for migrating my on-premises VMs to Azure? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="5c6dad44">
         <p>There are several Microsoft and partner tools and a large ecosystem of partners to help migrate on-premises VMs to Azure. <a href="/en-us/migration/">Visit the Azure migration center</a> to learn more.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="c10b8d36" data-bi-slot="11" data-bi-id="faq-11" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What are availability sets? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="c10b8d36">
         <p>Availability sets are logical grouping capabilities to ensure that VM resources placed within them are isolated from each other when they are deployed within an Azure datacenter.</p> 
         <p>Azure ensures that the VMs you place within availability sets run across multiple physical servers, compute racks, storage units, and network switches.</p> 
         <p>If a hardware or Azure software failure occurs, only a subset of your VMs will be impacted. Availability sets are an essential capability for building reliable cloud solutions. To provide redundancy to your application, it is recommended that you group two or more virtual machines in an availability set.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="09b7c557" data-bi-slot="12" data-bi-id="faq-12" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What SLAs are available for Azure VMs? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="09b7c557">
         Microsoft offers a range of OS-independent SLAs for Azure VMs. Read the <a href="/en-us/support/legal/sla/virtual-machines/">SLA for Azure Virtual Machines</a>.
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="2a6900f9" data-bi-slot="13" data-bi-id="faq-13" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What disk storage options do I have when I provision a new Azure VM? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="2a6900f9">
         <p>Most Azure VMs come with temporary non-persistent local storage. Additionally, Azure offers HDD and SSD storage for data. Learn more about <a href="/en-us/services/storage/disks/">Azure Disk Storage</a>. Read the technical documentation (for <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/sizes?toc=%2fazure%2fvirtual-machines%2flinux%2ftoc.json">Linux VMs</a> and <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/windows/sizes?toc=%2fazure%2fvirtual-machines%2fwindows%2ftoc.json">Windows VMs</a>) to learn about the Azure disks that are available for each VM series.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="bf481748" data-bi-slot="14" data-bi-id="faq-14" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Can I use my existing Windows Server or Linux Server licenses on Azure? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="bf481748">
         <p>As you transition your workloads to Azure, take advantage of <a href="/en-us/pricing/hybrid-benefit/">Azure Hybrid Benefit</a> to reuse your existing Windows Server licenses with Software Assurance or Windows Server subscriptions for significant savings. For each license, Azure covers the cost of the OS, while you pay for just the VM compute costs. Additionally, through Azure Hybrid Benefit for Linux, you can use your pre-existing on-premises Red Hat and SUSE software subscriptions on Azure. <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/virtual-machines/linux/azure-hybrid-benefit-linux">Learn more.</a></p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="954f8b95" data-bi-slot="15" data-bi-id="faq-15" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What are Azure Virtual Machine Scale Sets? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="954f8b95">
         <p><a href="/en-us/services/virtual-machine-scale-sets/">Virtual Machine Scale Sets</a> help you create and manage a group of load-balanced and autoscaling VMs. Deploy VM scale sets using Azure Resource Manager templates, which support Windows and Linux platform images and custom images and extensions.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="2118d278" data-bi-slot="16" data-bi-id="faq-16" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Can I try Azure before I buy? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="2118d278">
         <p>Of course. Create an <a href="/en-us/free/services/virtual-machines/">Azure free account</a> to learn how Azure works, try products and cloud services, and view tutorials on how to deploy your first solution in 10 minutes or less. <a href="/en-us/get-started/">Get started</a>.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="f9f14755" data-bi-slot="17" data-bi-id="faq-17" data-bi-an="faq-01"> How safe is my companys data in the cloud? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="f9f14755">
         <p>Security and privacy are built into the Azure platform. Microsoft is committed to the highest levels of trust, transparency, standards conformance, and regulatory compliance with the most comprehensive set of compliance offerings of any cloud service provider. <a href="https://www.microsoft.com/trustcenter/cloudservices/azure">Learn more</a>.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="f4b8ec1e" data-bi-slot="18" data-bi-id="faq-18" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Will Azure really save me money? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="f4b8ec1e">
         <p>With no upfront cost, you only pay for what you use. Azure provides flexible purchasing and pricing options for all your cloud scenarios, such as the Azure Hybrid Benefit and Azure Reserved Virtual Machine Instances. Azure also offers a comprehensive set of tools to help manage your cloud spend. <a href="/en-us/pricing/">Learn more</a>.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="c1f28969" data-bi-slot="19" data-bi-id="faq-19" data-bi-an="faq-01"> How does Azure compare to other cloud providers? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="c1f28969">
         <p>More than 95 percent of Fortune 500 companies use Azure. Azure has more global regions than any cloud provider and offers the most comprehensive set of compliance offerings. Azure offers built-in support for the most popular integrated development environments trusted by more than 20 million developersVisual Studio and Visual Studio Code. <a href="/en-us/overview/azure-vs-aws/">Compare Azure vs. AWS</a>.</p>
        </div> </li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section> 
   <section class="section section--image-offset " aria-label="Ready when you arelets set up your Azure free account." data-module="cta-band-portal-01"> 
    <div class="row row--middled-small"> 
     <div class="column medium-6 large-4"> 
      <div class="row column"> 
       <h2>Ready when you arelets set up your Azure free account.</h2> 
      </div>
